 do dinon main 35 baar golabari kii gai
 Let me tell you, there has been continuous firing from Pakistan since the Airstrike
 guuruuvaar ko saatven din bhi pakistan ne mortar daage

 guuruuvaar ko subah 6 baje se hi golabari shuru hui thi

 iskaa bhartiya sena ne dridhtaa or prabhavi dhang se jawaab diya

 usne pichley kareeb 2,936 baar golabari kii thi
 The official said that Pakistan is also seizing fire during the flag meeting between the border security forces of the two countries and promising to abide by the agreement
 maujuuda daur main jahaan kai paaramparik shilp apana astitv bachaane ke liye jaddojahad kar rahe hai, vahiin duusari ore gujarat ke kuccha main basaa ajrakhpur naamak chota sa gaanv gharelu or antarrashtriya kharidaaron ko apane prakritik chatkh rangon se range block prit kapadon se lubhaa rahaa he
 This print is known as Ajrakh, which takes a lot of time and effort to make and is a long process
 gaanv ke sau se adhik parivaar is shilp se jude hue hai, jiske baad ucchtam koti kaa kapadaa taiyaar hota he, or phir is par fishan kii sheersh company kaa label lagata he
 While the Chief Minister of Gujarat, Prime Minister Narendra Modi assured to promote the art of this village
 bhuj main 2001 main aae bheeshan bukamp ke baad dhamadaka gaanv se ajrakhpur main aakar based sufian ismail khatari ke mutabik, yah gaanv bahut purana nahin he, lekin unka yah shilp 400 varshon se adhik purana he
 Sufiyan Ajrakh is from the 9th generation of printers
 unhone apane purvajon kii us kala ko aaj tak sanjo kar rakhaa he, jise unke purvaj sindh se lekar yahaan aae the
 Teaching design to a craftsman, Sufiyan said, ‚Äútraditional Azrakh printing is a 16-step process through natural colors
 isamen 14 se 21 dinon kaa samay lagata he
 It also depends on how many colors will be in it and how many levels of block print will be used
 " The clothes are soaked overnight in water before dyeing them, so that excess starch comes out of them
 iske baad unhen dhoop main sukhaya jaataa he
 After drying they are dyed with Mayobralam color, after which they are again placed in the sun to dry
 is prakriya ke puraa hone ke baad shilpkaar paaramparik diginon vaale lakdi ke block ko chunate hai or phir unhen gond kii sahaayta se saavdhaneepurvak kapadon par chipkaaya jaataa he
 In Azrakh printing, after placing a block on the cloth, it has to be pressed
 isi prakaar shilpkaar blox ko chunate hai, unhen rangate hai or saavdhaneepurvak unhen kapadon par rakhkar dabaaya jaataa he
 After this process is completed, the clothes are washed and dried in the sun
 kapadon me istemaal hone vaali sabhi rang prakritik tareeke se banaae jate hai
 Ajrakh is called indigo in Arabic, which means the indigo plant
 yah paudha 1956 main kuccha main aae bukamp se pehle tak ilaake main har taraf dikhataa tha
 But, if some craftsmen are to be believed, the word Azrakh comes from 'aaj Rakh'
 ajrakhpur workshop ke aasapaas baari maatra main aapako lohe kaa chura dekhne ko milegaa
 Black color is made by mixing jaggery and gram flour in iron shred
 gaanv ke ek anya shilpkaar ismail anwar ne bataaya ki is rang ko banane main kam se kam 15 dinon kaa samay lagata he
 Red color is made from tamarind seeds and alum
 haldi se pilaa rang banaaya jaataa he or chooney kaa istemaal safed rang banane ke liye kiya jaataa he
 Anwar said, "traditionally, Azrakh printing was done only with natural colors, but now artificial colors are also used due to the demand for cheaper varieties
 kritrim rangon se kii gai pintring main kam samay lagata he
 " unhone bataaya ki kritrim pintring se ek sari ke taiyaar hone main do din kaa samay lagata he
 Whenever there is a high demand for goods, this is used
 kritrim rangon se taiyaar kiye gaye kapade kii keemat 50 se 60 rupye prati meter hoti he, par yadi kapade main anokhe dizin kaa print kiya gaya he, to uski keemat 100 rupye prati meter tak ja sakati he
 The story of Ajrakh was not always so colorful
 in shilpakaaron ke jivan main bhi ek bura samay aayaa tha, jab sabhi shilpakaaron ko apana sab kuch chhodkar duusari jagah janaa padaa or jivan jeene ke liye phir se sabhi sansadhano ko jhonkkar sabakuch dobaaraa shuru karnaa padaa
 Sufiyan said, 'today our craft is in great demand in the market
 tarun tahaliani jaise diziner ne mere saath kaam kiya he
 At the invitation of the designers, i got opportunities to go to different places and show my art
 aaj duniya ke bade-bade diziner hamaari kala ke bare main jaananaa chaahate hai
 " anwar ne bataaya ki diziner institute se bahut se bachche unki kala ko seekhney ke liye aate hai
 Artisans from all over the world come to see his exhibition
 unhone kaha ki unka yah kaam kisi bhi mausam main rukta nahin he, chaahe sardi ho yaa garmi
 His work continues in the hot summer of April as it is the best time to work
 tippaniyan Anwar's nephew, who works in the workshop, said that our workmanship is everything to us
 hamaari yah kala peedi dar peedi se chali aa rahi he
 People's love for Ajrakh is the biggest gift for us
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) According to Sufiyan Ismail Khatri, who settled in Ajrakpur from Dhamdaka village after the devastating earthquake in Bhuj in 2001, this village is not very old, but his craft is more than 400 years old
 sufian ajrakh printer kii 9veen peedi se hai
 They have preserved the art of their ancestors till date, which their ancestors brought here from Sindh
 ek shilpkaar ko dizin sikhaate hue sufian ne kaha, "prakritik rangon ke madhyam se paaramparik ajrakh priting 16 charnon kii prakriya he
 It takes 14 to 21 days
 yah is baat par bhi nirbhar karata he ki isamen kitne rang honge or block print ke kitne staron kaa istemaal kiya jayega
 " kapadon ko daai karne se pehle unhen pani main puri raat bhigoya jaataa he, taaki unamem se atirikt starch nikal jaae
 They are then dried in the sun
 sookhne ke baad unhen mayobralam rang se ranga jaataa he, jiske baad phir se unhen dhoop main sookhne ke liye rakh diya jaataa he
 After the completion of this process, craftsmen choose wooden blocks with traditional designs and then glue them carefully onto the cloth with the help of glue
 ajrakh printig main kapade par block rakhane ke baad use dabaakar rakhana hota he
 Similarly, craftsmen choose blocks, color them and carefully place them on clothes and press them
 yah prakriya puri hone ke baad kapadon ko dhokar dhoop main sukhaya jaataa he
 All the colors used in clothes are made in a natural way
 ajrakh ko arabi bhashaa main indigo kaha jaataa he, jiskaa arth nil kaa paudha hota he
 This plant was visible everywhere in the area before the 1956 earthquake in Kutch
 lekin, kuch shilpakaaron kii maane to ajrakh shabd 'aaj rakh' se aayaa he
 You will see a large amount of iron sawdust around the Ajrakhpur workshop
 lohe ke chure main gud or besan milakar kaala rang banaaya jaataa he
 Another craftsman from the village, Ismail Anwar, said that it takes at least 15 days to make this color
 imali ke beej or fitkaree se laal rang banaaya jaataa he
 Turmeric is a yellow color and lime is used to make white
 anwar ne kaha, "paramparaagat rup se ajrakh printig keval prakritik rangon se hi kii jaati thi, lekin ab sasti kism kii maang ke chalate isamen kritrim rangon kaa bhi istemaal kiya jaataa he
 Pintering done with artificial colors takes less time
 " He said that it takes two days to prepare a saree with artificial pintering
 jab kabhi maal kii zyada maang hoti he, to isi kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
 a fabric made of artificial colors costs 50 to 60 rupees per meter, but if the fabric is printed with a unique design, then the price can go up to 100 rupees per meter
 ajrakh kii kahani hameshaa se itani rangarang nahin thi
 There was also a bad time in the lives of these craftsmen, when all the craftsmen had to give up everything and move to another place and start living life again and put all the resources back
 sufian ne bataaya, 'aaj hamaare shilp kii bazaar main bahut maang he
 Designers like Tarun Tahiliani have worked with me
 diziners ke aamantran par mujhe alag-alag jagah jaakar apni kala dikhaane ke maukey mili
 Today, big designers of the world want to know about our art
 " Anwar said that many children come from the designer institute to learn their art
 duniyabar ke sabhi karigar unki pradarshnee dekhne aate hai
 He said that his work does not stop in any season, whether it is winter or summer
 unka yah kaam april maheene kii tej garmi main bhi chalata rahata he, kyonki kaam karne ke liye yah sabase acha samay hota he
 The comments workshop main kaam karne vaale anwar ke bhattije ne bataaya ki hamaari kaarigari hi hamaare liye sabakuch he
 This art of ours has been going on from generation to generation
 logon kaa ajrakh ke prati pyaar hi hamaare liye sabase bada tohfa he

 1

 self diagnostic system and temper ditection progaam bhi shaamil hai
 2

 3

 6
 hamaari iviem sabase aage he, jiskaa data aantarik taur par sef he

 Important Books for the preparation of UPSC (IAS) Prelims: 1
 em
 The book, Indian Politics for Civil Services Examinations written by Laxmikant (politics), needs no introduction
 ye iklauti kitaab he jo aapaki taiyaari kaa puraa najariya hi badal sakati he
 This book is recommended by most all IAS toppers
 aaj ye vibhinn pratiyogi parikshaon or khaskar civil seva pariksha ke ummidavaaron ke liye ek jarur se jarur padhi jane vaali pustak ban gai he
 2
 nitin singhania (culture) kii likhi kitabaindian art and cultumbhartiya viraasat or samskruti ke puure paathyakram ko samajhane ke liye ek jaruri kitaab he
 There are also many questions that help in the preparation of the exam
 3
 The Certificate Physical and Human Geographie written by Goh Cheng Leong (geography) is the best-seller book that every UPSC IAS topper remembers
 kitaab main puure bhugol paathyakram ko shaamil kiya gaya he jo aapke upiessi praarambhik or mukhya pariksha ke liye jaruri he
 Apart from this, NCERT books from class 6-12 are also helpful in preparation
 4
 Oxford School Atlas (geography) UPSC candidates must read this book by Oxford Publishers
 isamen bharat ke 94 vishaygat maanchitron ke saath 200 maanchitr shaamil hai
 5
 ramesh singh (arthvyavastha) kii likhi indian iconamirmesh singh kii likhi iconomics kii is kitaab main puraa comprehensive text diya he
 It covers every subject in detail
 6
 Economic Survey by Ministry (economy) Economic survey by Ministry of Finance is the most reliable data source of India's economy
 yah kitaab sarkaar kii niti or pradarshan ke bare main puri jaankaree detaa he
 7
 india year bukye ek aisi riference book he jisamen desh kaa puraa curent afares aasaani se pataa lag jaataa he or ye ek aadhikarik sankalan he
 It contains important data related to important dignitaries, state policy, public plans and demographics, trade, economy and more
 8
 Brief History of Modern India written by Rajiv Ahir (modern India)
 Brief History of Modern India written by Indira Rajeev Ahir deals with events that are related to the fall of the Mughal Empire and the rise of the East India Company
 isamen desh main british shashan ke aagaman ke baad ghatit hui ghatnaayen hai
